Req-496: before the steering wheel angle whose index is greater than 5 is greater than the sailing termination for 4 seconds , if the steering wheel angle that equals 8 equals [False] within 10 seconds , when the NoSailing requests exceeds the vehicle speed quality factor for 3 seconds every at least 13 seconds ,  the engine error shall be received from the brake fault state  within 11 seconds  .
[
comp( 
[ 
subComp(condScope, Nil, before, the steering wheel angle, is greater than, [the sailing termination, ], before the steering wheel angle is greater than the sailing termination ),
subComp(hidden, the steering wheel angle, whose, index, is greater than, [5, ], the steering wheel angle whose index is greater than 5 ),
subComp(v-time, for, , 4, seconds, [], for 4 seconds)
] ),

comp( 
[ 
subComp(cond, Nil, if, the steering wheel angle, equals, [[False], ], if the steering wheel angle equals [False] ),
subComp(hidden, the steering wheel angle, that, Nil, equals, [8, ], the steering wheel angle that equals 8 ),
subComp(pre-time, within, , 10, seconds, [], within 10 seconds)
] ),

comp( 
[ 
subComp(ttrig, Nil, when, the NoSailing requests, exceeds, [the vehicle speed quality factor, ], when the NoSailing requests exceeds the vehicle speed quality factor ),
subComp(v-time, for, , 3, seconds, [], for 3 seconds),
subComp(in-time, every, at least, 13, seconds, [], every at least 13 seconds)
] ),

comp( 
[ 
subComp(act, Nil, Nil, the engine error, shall be received, [the brake fault state, ], the engine error shall be received from the brake fault state),
subComp(pre-time, within, , 11, seconds, [], within 11 seconds)
] )

]

] ),

[ 
subComp(act, Nil, Nil, the brake fault state, shall be moved, [], the brake fault state shall be moved up),

] ),

[ 
subComp(cond, Nil, if, the IDC inhibitor, is above, [the standstill request flag, ], if the IDC inhibitor is above the standstill request flag ),

] )
